<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ведомо.html>ведомо</a> (11575)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>ве́домый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">védomyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Predicative">Predicative</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведомо.html>ве́домо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">védomo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> it is known
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ведомо.html>ве́домо</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вам</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:случиться.html>случи́лось</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>védomo</b> li vam, što slučílosʹ?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">do you know what happened?</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">is it known to you, what happened?</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одному́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бо́гу</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ведомо.html>ве́домо</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">odnomú Bógu <b>védomo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">God alone knows</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">it is known to God alone</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ведомость.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ведомость.html>ве́домость</a> (7808)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>ве́домый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">védomyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">known, familiar</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p><p>Compare to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">wiadomość</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">message, information, news</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведомость.html>ве́домость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">védomostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведомость.html>ве́домости</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведомость.html>ве́домости</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведомость.html>ве́домостей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>list, register, roll
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:платежный.html>платёжная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ведомость.html>ве́домость</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">platjóžnaja <b>védomostʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">paysheet, payroll</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gazette, bulletin</li></ol>

***ведро.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ведро.html>ведро́</a> (2078)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">вѣдро</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vědro</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vědro</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">water bucket</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wódr̥</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">water</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> root <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wed-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Classical_Armenian" class="extiw" title="w:Classical Armenian">Old Armenian</a></span> <i class="Armn mention" lang="xcl">գետ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xcl-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">get</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">river</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведро.html>ведро́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vedró</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведро.html>ведра́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведро.html>вёдра</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведро.html>вёдер</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bucket, pail
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дождь.html>дождь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лить.html>льёт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ведро.html>ведра́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">doždʹ lʹjót kak iz <b>vedrá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">it is raining cats and dogs</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>vedro; an ancient Russian measure of liquids equal to 12.3 liters (1/40 <a href = vnd.unilang:бочок.html>бочки</a>)</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vestí</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to lead</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведущий.html>веду́щий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vedúščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведущий.html>веду́щий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vedúščij</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведущий.html>веду́щего</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведущий.html>веду́щие</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведущий.html>веду́щих</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведущий.html>веду́щая</a></b>)

***ведь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ведь.html>ведь</a> (114)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">вѣдѣ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vědě</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Russian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведь.html>ведь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vedʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is a former <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> root perfect <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wóyde</i> with mediopassive ending <i>-ai</i>, with meaning "I have seen". Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wit</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведь.html>ведь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vedʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>after all</li>
<li>indeed, surely</li>
<li>why, well</li>
<li>then, you know, you see</li>
<li>isn’t it?
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ведь.html>Ведь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:уже.html>уже́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поздно.html>по́здно</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Vedʹ</b> užé pózdno</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It’s late, isn’t it?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ведь.html>Ведь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знаток.html>знато́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Vedʹ</b> on znatók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">After all, he’s an expert.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ведь.html>Ведь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́л</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Vedʹ</b> ja vam govoríl!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">But I told you!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведь.html>ведь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vedʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>you see, you know
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лежать.html>лежи́т</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ведь.html>ведь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прошлый.html>про́шлой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неделя.html>неде́ле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:заболеть.html>заболе́л</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On ležít, <b>vedʹ</b> on na próšloj nedéle zabolél</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He’s in bed...he fell ill last week, you know.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ведьма.html>ве́дьма</a> (2891)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">вѣдьма</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vědĭma</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vědьma</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведьма.html>ве́дьма</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">védʹma</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведьма.html>ве́дьмы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведьма.html>ве́дьмы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведьма.html>ве́дьм</a></b>)

***ведьмак.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ведьмак.html>ведьма́к</a> (31158)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведьма.html>ве́дьма</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">védʹma</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">witch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ák</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*věděti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to know</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведьмак.html>ведьма́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vedʹmák</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведьмак.html>ведьмака́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведьмак.html>ведьмаки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведьмак.html>ведьмако́в</a></b>)
</p>

***вежливый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вежливый.html>ве́жливый</a> (5148)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">вѣжливои</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">věžlivoi</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">experienced, versed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself from <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">вѣжливои</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">věžlivoi</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">knower, competent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*věďa</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*věděti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to know</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">невѣжда</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nevěžda</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ignorant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ливый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-livyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вездеход.html>вездехо́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vezdexód</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вездеход.html>вездехо́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вездеход.html>вездехо́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вездеход.html>вездехо́дов</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вез-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vez-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***везти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:везти.html>везти́</a> (1884)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vezti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*weǵʰ-</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">veho</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:везти.html>везти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">veztí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повезти.html>повезти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to convey, to carry (by vehicle), to deliver, to transport</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal verb</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be lucky, to have luck, to work out for, to succeed, to be successful (+ dative case)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">па́ше <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:саше.html>са́ше</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:везти.html>везёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Páše i Sáše ne <b>vezjót</b> sevódnja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Pasha and Sasha are having no luck today.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурак.html>дурака́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:всегда.html>всегда́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:везти.html>везёт</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">durakám vsegdá <b>vezjót</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">fools are always lucky</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повезти.html>повезти́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poveztí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:везти.html>Везти́</a></b> is a concrete verb. Its counterpart, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возить.html>вози́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vozítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, is an abstract verb.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:транспортировать.html>транспорти́ровать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">transportírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удачливый.html>уда́чливый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">udáčlivyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lucky</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***веко.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:веко.html>ве́ко</a> (4397)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*věko</i>.

***веление.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:веление.html>веле́ние</a> (21016)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:велеть.html>веле́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">velétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веление.html>веле́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">velénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веление.html>веле́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веление.html>веле́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:веление.html>веле́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>order, decree, injunction, behest
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>По</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:щучий.html>щу́чьему</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:веление.html>веле́нию</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотение.html>хоте́нию</a>.</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">an idiom from a <a href = vnd.unilang:поп.html>popular</a> fairy-tale, used sarcastically when something is expected to happen as if by a wave of a magic wand.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Po ščúčʹjemu <b>veléniju</b>, po mojemú xoténiju.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">By magic, by my desire. (By a pike's behest, by my desire)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***велеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:велеть.html>веле́ть</a> (1136)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*velě̀ti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*welh₁-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:велеть.html>веле́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">velétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повелеть.html>повеле́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to order (to do something), to enjoin, to command.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>Сам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>бог</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:велеть.html>веле́л</a></b>.</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">expression</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Sam box <b>velél</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">God Himself has <b>commanded</b> (it). <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">i.e. it's natural or allowed to do so</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>with <i>dative case</i> and <i>infinitive</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ей</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:велеть.html>веле́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>прийти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On jej <b>velél</b> prijtí sevódnja.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He commanded her to come today.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>The verb can be both perfective and imperfective, although in the past tense and infinitive it is predominantly perfective.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приказывать.html>прика́зывать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prikázyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> / <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приказать.html>приказа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prikazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повелевать.html>повелева́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">povelevátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:повелеть.html>повеле́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">povelétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***великий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:великий.html>вели́кий</a> (376)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*velikъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:великий.html>вели́кий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">velíkij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:более.html>бо́лее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:великий.html>вели́кий</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:величайший.html>велича́йший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>large, big</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">short form only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> too big; larger than necessary
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сапог.html>сапоги́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>велики́</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éti sapogí mne <b>velikí</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">These boots are too big for me.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>great, outstanding</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>A special short form is found in the expression <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>ма́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>вели́ка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot <b>mála</b> do velíka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">all ages</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">from small to big</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Here <b><a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>ма́ла</a></b> and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>вели́ка</a></b> are old short genitives.</li></ul>
